    10 // 支持的文件格式
    11 const ACCEPTED_TYPES: Record<string, string> = {
    12   'application/pdf': 'PDF',
    13   'application/msword': 'DOC',
    14   'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document': 'DOCX',
    15   'text/csv': 'CSV',
    16   'application/vnd.ms-excel': 'XLS',
    17   'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet': 'XLSX',
    18   'text/plain': 'TXT',
    19 };
    20 const ACCEPTED_EXTENSIONS = ['.pdf', '.doc', '.docx', '.csv', '.xls', '.xlsx', '.txt'];
    21 const MAX_SIZE_MB = 10;
    22 const MAX_SIZE_BYTES = MAX_SIZE_MB * 1024 * 1024;
    23 
    24 interface UploadState {
    25   status: 'idle' | 'uploading' | 'success' | 'error';
    26   progress: number;
    27   fileName: string;
    28   errorMsg: string;
    29 }
    30 
    31 interface ResumeUploaderProps {
    32   resumeId: string;
    33   onUploadComplete: (fileUrl: string, fileName: string, fileSize: number, fileType: string) => void;
    34 }
    35 
    36 export function ResumeUploader({ resumeId, onUploadComplete }: ResumeUploaderProps) {
    37   const { user } = useAuth();
    38   const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);
    39   const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
    40   const [uploadState, setUploadState] = useState<UploadState>({
    41     status: 'idle', progress: 0, fileName: '', errorMsg: '',
    42   });
    43 
    44   const validateFile = (file: File): string | null => {
    45     const mimeOk = Object.keys(ACCEPTED_TYPES).includes(file.type);
    46     const extOk = ACCEPTED_EXTENSIONS.some(ext =>
    47       file.name.toLowerCase().endsWith(ext)
    48     );
    49     if (!mimeOk && !extOk) {
    50       return `不支持该文件格式，请上传 ${ACCEPTED_EXTENSIONS.join(' / ')} 格式的文件`;
    51     }
    52     if (file.size > MAX_SIZE_BYTES) {
    53       return `文件大小不能超过 ${MAX_SIZE_MB}MB（当前 ${(file.size / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(1)}MB）`;
    54     }
    55     return null;
    56   };
    57 
    58   const uploadFile = useCallback(async (file: File) => {
    59     if (!user) return;
    60 
    61     const validationError = validateFile(file);
    62     if (validationError) {
    63       setUploadState({ status: 'error', progress: 0, fileName: file.name, errorMsg: validationError });
    64       return;
    65     }
    66 
    67     setUploadState({ status: 'uploading', progress: 5, fileName: file.name, errorMsg: '' });
    68 
    69     // 构造文件路径：user_id/resume_id/filename（保证唯一性）
    70     const ext = file.name.substring(file.name.lastIndexOf('.'));
    71     const safeName = file.name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9._\u4e00-\u9fa5-]/g, '_');
    72     const filePath = `${user.id}/${resumeId}/${Date.now()}_${safeName}`;
    73 
    74     // 模拟进度 - Supabase 客户端上传不暴露进度回调，用定时器模拟
    75     let fakeProgress = 5;
    76     const progressTimer = setInterval(() => {
    77       fakeProgress = Math.min(fakeProgress + Math.random() * 15, 85);
    78       setUploadState(prev => ({ ...prev, progress: Math.round(fakeProgress) }));
    79     }, 200);
    80 
    81     const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
    82       .from('resumes')
    83       .upload(filePath, file, {
    84         cacheControl: '3600',
    85         upsert: false,
    86         contentType: file.type || 'application/octet-stream',
    87       });
    88 
    89     clearInterval(progressTimer);
    90 
    91     if (uploadError) {
    92       setUploadState({
    93         status: 'error', progress: 0, fileName: file.name,
    94         errorMsg: uploadError.message || '文件上传失败，请重试',
    95       });
    96       toast.error('文件上传失败');
    97       return;
    98     }
    99 
   100     // 获取私有文件的签名 URL（有效期1年）
   101     const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
   102       .from('resumes')
   103       .createSignedUrl(filePath, 60 * 60 * 24 * 365);
   104 
   105     if (urlError || !urlData) {
   106       setUploadState({
   107         status: 'error', progress: 0, fileName: file.name,
   108         errorMsg: '获取文件链接失败',
   109       });
   110       return;
   111     }
   112 
   113     setUploadState({ status: 'success', progress: 100, fileName: file.name, errorMsg: '' });
   114     toast.success('文件上传成功');
   115 
   116     const fileType = ACCEPTED_TYPES[file.type] || ext.replace('.', '').toUpperCase();
   117     onUploadComplete(urlData.signedUrl, file.name, file.size, fileType);
   118   }, [user, resumeId, onUploadComplete]);
   119 
   120   // 拖拽处理
   121   const handleDragOver = (e: React.DragEvent) => {
   122     e.preventDefault();
   123     setIsDragging(true);
   124   };
   125   const handleDragLeave = () => setIsDragging(false);
   126   const handleDrop = (e: React.DragEvent) => {
   127     e.preventDefault();
   128     setIsDragging(false);
   129     const file = e.dataTransfer.files[0];
   130     if (file) uploadFile(file);
   131   };
   132   const handleFileChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
   133     const file = e.target.files?.[0];
   134     if (file) uploadFile(file);
   135     // 清空 input 以允许重复选同一文件
   136     e.target.value = '';
   137   };
   138 
   139   const handleReset = () => {
   140     setUploadState({ status: 'idle', progress: 0, fileName: '', errorMsg: '' });
   141   };
   142 
   143   return (
   144     <div className="space-y-3">
   145       {/* 拖拽区域 */}
   146       {uploadState.status === 'idle' && (
   147         <div
   148           onDragOver={handleDragOver}
   149           onDragLeave={handleDragLeave}
   150           onDrop={handleDrop}
   151           onClick={() => inputRef.current?.click()}
   152           className={cn(
   153             'relative border-2 border-dashed rounded-lg p-6 text-center cursor-pointer transition-colors select-none',
   154             isDragging
   155               ? 'border-primary bg-primary/5'
   156               : 'border-border hover:border-primary/50 hover:bg-muted/30'
   157           )}
   158         >
   159           <Upload className={cn(
   160             'w-8 h-8 mx-auto mb-3 transition-colors',
   161             isDragging ? 'text-primary' : 'text-muted-foreground'
   162           )} />
   163           <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">
   164             {isDragging ? '松开鼠标上传文件' : '拖拽文件至此，或点击选择文件'}
   165           </p>
   166           <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1.5">
   167             支持 PDF · Word（DOC/DOCX）· CSV · Excel · TXT，最大 {MAX_SIZE_MB}MB
   168           </p>
   169           <input
   170             ref={inputRef}
   171             type="file"
   172             accept={ACCEPTED_EXTENSIONS.join(',')}
   173             className="hidden"
   174             onChange={handleFileChange}
   175           />
   176         </div>
   177       )}
   178 
   179       {/* 上传中 */}
   180       {uploadState.status === 'uploading' && (
   181         <div className="border border-border rounded-lg p-4 space-y-3">
   182           <div className="flex items-center gap-3 min-w-0">
   183             <FileText className="w-5 h-5 text-primary shrink-0" />
   184             <span className="text-sm text-foreground truncate flex-1 min-w-0">
   185               {uploadState.fileName}
   186             </span>
   187             <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground shrink-0">{uploadState.progress}%</span>
   188           </div>
   189           <Progress value={uploadState.progress} className="h-1.5" />
   190           <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">正在上传，请稍候…</p>
   191         </div>
   192       )}
   193 
   194       {/* 上传成功 */}
   195       {uploadState.status === 'success' && (
   196         <div className="border border-primary/30 bg-primary/5 rounded-lg p-4 flex items-center gap-3">
   197           <CheckCircle2 className="w-5 h-5 text-primary shrink-0" />
   198           <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
   199             <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground truncate">{uploadState.fileName}</p>
   200             <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">上传成功</p>
   201           </div>
   202           <Button
   203             variant="ghost"
   204             size="icon"
   205             className="h-7 w-7 shrink-0 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
   206             onClick={handleReset}
   207             title="重新上传"
   208           >
   209             <X className="w-4 h-4" />
   210           </Button>
   211         </div>
   212       )}
   213 
   214       {/* 上传失败 */}
   215       {uploadState.status === 'error' && (
   216         <div className="border border-destructive/30 bg-destructive/5 rounded-lg p-4 space-y-2">
   217           <div className="flex items-center gap-3 min-w-0">
   218             <AlertCircle className="w-5 h-5 text-destructive shrink-0" />
   219             <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground truncate flex-1 min-w-0">
   220               {uploadState.fileName || '文件上传失败'}
   221             </p>
   222           </div>
   223           <p className="text-xs text-destructive pl-8">{uploadState.errorMsg}</p>
   224           <div className="pl-8">
   225             <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="h-7 text-xs" onClick={handleReset}>
   226               重新选择
   227             </Button>
   228           </div>
   229         </div>
   230       )}
   231     </div>
   232   );
   233 }

    41 function formatFileSize(bytes?: number): string {
    42   if (!bytes) return '未知大小';
    43   if (bytes < 1024) return `${bytes} B`;
    44   if (bytes < 1024 * 1024) return `${(bytes / 1024).toFixed(1)} KB`;
    45   return `${(bytes / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(1)} MB`;
    46 }

    48 const DEFAULT_RADAR_DATA = [
    49   { subject: '编程技能', value: 75 },

    66 export default function ResumeManagement() {
    67   const { user } = useAuth();
    68   const [resumes, setResumes] = useState<Resume[]>([]);
    69   const [capability, setCapability] = useState<CapabilityData | null>(null);
    70   const [templates, setTemplates] = useState<IndustryTemplate[]>([]);
    71   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    72   const [radarData, setRadarData] = useState(DEFAULT_RADAR_DATA);
    73   const [addDialogOpen, setAddDialogOpen] = useState(false);
    74   const [newResumeTitle, setNewResumeTitle] = useState('');
    75   const [selectedIndustry, setSelectedIndustry] = useState('tech');
    76   // 当前正在上传文件的简历 ID
    77   const [uploadingResumeId, setUploadingResumeId] = useState<string | null>(null);
    78 
    79   useEffect(() => {
    80     if (user) {
    81       fetchResumes();
    82       fetchCapabilityData();
    83       fetchTemplates();
    84     }
    85   }, [user]);
    86 
    87   const fetchResumes = async () => {
    88     const { data } = await supabase
    89       .from('resumes')
    90       .select('*')
    91       .eq('profile_id', user!.id)
    92       .order('created_at', { ascending: false });
    93     setResumes(Array.isArray(data) ? data as Resume[] : []);
    94     setLoading(false);
    95   };
    96 
    97   const fetchCapabilityData = async () => {
    98     const { data } = await supabase
    99       .from('capability_data')
   100       .select('*')
   101       .eq('profile_id', user!.id)
   102       .maybeSingle();
   103     if (data) {
   104       setCapability(data as CapabilityData);
   105       const rd = data.radar_data as Record<string, number>;
   106       if (rd && Object.keys(rd).length > 0) {
   107         setRadarData(Object.entries(rd).map(([subject, value]) => ({ subject, value })));
   108       }
   109     }
   110   };
   111 
   112   const fetchTemplates = async () => {
   113     const { data } = await supabase.from('industry_templates').select('*').order('label');
   114     setTemplates(Array.isArray(data) ? data as IndustryTemplate[] : []);
   115   };
   116 
   117   const handleAddResume = async () => {
   118     if (!newResumeTitle.trim()) return;
   119     const { data, error } = await supabase
   120       .from('resumes')
   121       .insert({
   122         profile_id: user!.id,
   123         title: newResumeTitle,
   124         is_primary: resumes.length === 0,
   125       })
   126       .select()
   127       .maybeSingle();
   128     if (error) { toast.error('创建简历失败'); return; }
   129     toast.success('简历已创建，可立即上传文件');
   130     setAddDialogOpen(false);
   131     setNewResumeTitle('');
   132     // 创建后自动展开上传区
   133     if (data?.id) setUploadingResumeId(data.id);
   134     fetchResumes();
   135   };
   136 
   137   const handleDeleteResume = async (resume: Resume) => {
   138     // 若有附件先从 Storage 删除
   139     if (resume.file_url && resume.file_name) {
   140       const filePath = `${user!.id}/${resume.id}`;
   141       await supabase.storage.from('resumes').remove([filePath]);
   142     }
   143     const { error } = await supabase.from('resumes').delete().eq('id', resume.id);
   144     if (error) { toast.error('删除失败'); return; }
   145     toast.success('简历已删除');
   146     if (uploadingResumeId === resume.id) setUploadingResumeId(null);
   147     fetchResumes();
   148   };
   149 
   150   const handleSetPrimary = async (id: string) => {
   151     await supabase.from('resumes').update({ is_primary: false }).eq('profile_id', user!.id);
   152     await supabase.from('resumes').update({ is_primary: true }).eq('id', id);
   153     fetchResumes();
   154     toast.success('已设为主简历');
   155   };
   156 
   157   // 上传完成回调 —— 更新数据库中的文件字段
   158   const handleUploadComplete = async (
   159     resumeId: string,
   160     fileUrl: string,
   161     fileName: string,
   162     fileSize: number,
   163     fileType: string,
   164   ) => {
   165     const { error } = await supabase
   166       .from('resumes')
   167       .update({
   168         file_url: fileUrl,
   169         file_name: fileName,
   170         file_size: fileSize,
   171         file_type: fileType,
   172         uploaded_at: new Date().toISOString(),
   173       })
   174       .eq('id', resumeId);
   175     if (error) { toast.error('文件信息保存失败'); return; }
   176     setUploadingResumeId(null);
   177     fetchResumes();
   178   };
   179 
   180   const handleDownload = async (resume: Resume) => {
   181     if (!resume.file_url) return;
   182     try {
   183       const link = document.createElement('a');
   184       link.href = resume.file_url;
   185       link.download = resume.file_name || '简历文件';
   186       link.target = '_blank';
   187       link.rel = 'noopener noreferrer';
   188       document.body.appendChild(link);
   189       link.click();
   190       document.body.removeChild(link);
   191     } catch {
   192       toast.error('下载失败，请重试');
   193     }
   194   };
   195 
   196   const handleSaveCapability = async () => {
   197     const radarObj: Record<string, number> = {};
   198     radarData.forEach(item => { radarObj[item.subject] = item.value; });
   199 
   200     const currentTemplate = templates.find(t => t.industry === selectedIndustry);
   201     const treeData = currentTemplate ? currentTemplate.skill_tree : DEFAULT_TREE;
   202 
   203     if (capability) {
   204       await supabase.from('capability_data')
   205         .update({ radar_data: radarObj, tree_data: treeData, industry: selectedIndustry })
   206         .eq('id', capability.id);
   207     } else {
   208       await supabase.from('capability_data').insert({
   209         profile_id: user!.id,
   210         industry: selectedIndustry,
   211         radar_data: radarObj,
   212         tree_data: treeData,
   213         skills: radarData.map(r => ({ name: r.subject, level: r.value })),
   214       });
   215     }
   216     toast.success('能力数据已保存');
   217     fetchCapabilityData();
   218   };
   219 
   220   const currentTemplate = templates.find(t => t.industry === selectedIndustry);
   221   const treeData = (capability?.tree_data && Object.keys(capability.tree_data).length > 0)
   222     ? capability.tree_data
   223     : currentTemplate?.skill_tree || DEFAULT_TREE;
   224 
   225   return (
   226     <div className="max-w-5xl mx-auto px-4 md:px-8 py-6 space-y-6">
   227       <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
   228         <h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-foreground text-balance">简历管理</h1>
   229         <Dialog open={addDialogOpen} onOpenChange={setAddDialogOpen}>

    21 const CustomTooltip = ({ active, payload }: { active?: boolean; payload?: Array<{ value: number; name: string }> }) => {
    22   if (active && payload && payload.length) {
    23     return (
    24       <div className="bg-card border border-border rounded-md px-3 py-2 shadow-sm text-sm">

    27             <span className="text-muted-foreground">{p.name}:</span>
    28             <span className="font-medium">{p.value}</span>
    29           </div>
    30         ))}
    31       </div>
    32     );
    33   }
    34   return null;
    35 };

    37 export function CapabilityRadarChart({
    38   data,

    44   const mergedData = data.map((item, i) => ({

    46     个人能力: item.value,

     1 import React, { useState } from 'react';
     2 import { TreeNode } from '@/types/types';
     3 import { ChevronRight, ChevronDown, Circle } from 'lucide-react';
     4 
     5 interface CapabilityTreeChartProps {
     6   data: TreeNode;
     7   depth?: number;
     8 }
     9 
    10 interface TreeNodeItemProps {
    11   node: TreeNode;
    12   depth: number;
    13   expanded?: boolean;
    14 }
    15 
    16 function TreeNodeItem({ node, depth }: TreeNodeItemProps) {
    17   const [isExpanded, setIsExpanded] = useState(depth < 2);
    18   const hasChildren = node.children && node.children.length > 0;
    19   const indent = depth * 20;
    20 
    21   const getNodeColor = () => {
    22     if (depth === 0) return 'text-primary font-semibold text-base';
    23     if (depth === 1) return 'text-foreground font-medium';
    24     return 'text-muted-foreground text-sm';
    25   };
    26 
    27   const getBarColor = () => {
    28     if (node.value === undefined) return null;
    29     if (node.value >= 80) return 'bg-primary';
    30     if (node.value >= 60) return 'bg-chart-2';
    31     if (node.value >= 40) return 'bg-chart-4';
    32     return 'bg-muted-foreground';
    33   };
    34 
    35   return (
    36     <div>
    37       <div
    38         className={`flex items-center gap-2 py-1.5 rounded-sm hover:bg-muted/50 cursor-pointer transition-colors ${hasChildren ? '' : 'cursor-default'}`}
    39         style={{ paddingLeft: `${indent + 8}px` }}
    40         onClick={() => hasChildren && setIsExpanded(v => !v)}
    41       >
    42         <span className="shrink-0 w-4 h-4 flex items-center justify-center">
    43           {hasChildren ? (
    44             isExpanded ? <ChevronDown className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground" /> : <ChevronRight className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground" />
    45           ) : (
    46             <Circle className="w-2 h-2 text-muted-foreground fill-muted-foreground" />
    47           )}
    48         </span>
    49         <span className={`flex-1 min-w-0 truncate ${getNodeColor()}`}>{node.name}</span>
    50         {node.value !== undefined && (
    51           <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0">
    52             <div className="w-20 h-1.5 bg-muted rounded-full overflow-hidden">
    53               <div
    54                 className={`h-full rounded-full transition-all ${getBarColor()}`}
    55                 style={{ width: `${node.value}%` }}
    56               />
    57             </div>
    58             <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground w-7 text-right">{node.value}</span>
    59           </div>
    60         )}
    61       </div>
    62       {hasChildren && isExpanded && (
    63         <div>
    64           {node.children!.map((child, i) => (
    65             <TreeNodeItem key={i} node={child} depth={depth + 1} />
    66           ))}
    67         </div>
    68       )}
    69     </div>
    70   );
    71 }
    72 
    73 export function CapabilityTreeChart({ data, depth = 0 }: CapabilityTreeChartProps) {
    74   return (
    75     <div className="w-full">
    76       <TreeNodeItem node={data} depth={depth} />
    77     </div>
    78   );

    32 export default function JobSearch() {

    43   const fetchJobs = async (search?: string) => {

    47       .select('*')

    55       const [min, max] = salaryRange.split('-').map(Number);
    56       if (min) query = query.gte('salary_min', min);
    57       if (max < 999999) query = query.lte('salary_max', max);
    58     }
    59

    61     if (error) toast.error('加载失败');

    75     return `最高${max! / 1000}k`;
    76   };

    83       <Card>

    85           <form onSubmit={handleSearch} className="flex gap-2">
    86             <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 relative">
    87               <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
    88               <Input
    89                 placeholder="搜索职位名称、技能关键词..."
    90                 value={searchText}
    91                 onChange={e => setSearchText(e.target.value)}
    92                 className="pl-9 px-3"
    93               />
    94             </div>
    95             <Button type="submit" size="sm" className="shrink-0 h-9">搜索</Button>
    96           </form>
    97           <div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap">
    98             <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-sm text-muted-foreground shrink-0">
    99               <Filter className="w-4 h-4" />筛选:
   100             </div>
   101             <Select value={industry} onValueChange={setIndustry}>
   102               <SelectTrigger className="w-36 h-8 text-sm">
   103                 <SelectValue />
   104               </SelectTrigger>
   105               <SelectContent>
   106                 {INDUSTRIES.map(i => (
   107                   <SelectItem key={i.value} value={i.value}>{i.label}</SelectItem>
   108                 ))}
   109               </SelectContent>
   110             </Select>
   111             <Select value={salaryRange} onValueChange={setSalaryRange}>
   112               <SelectTrigger className="w-36 h-8 text-sm">
   113                 <SelectValue />
   114               </SelectTrigger>
   115               <SelectContent>
   116                 {SALARY_RANGES.map(s => (
   117                   <SelectItem key={s.value} value={s.value}>{s.label}</SelectItem>
   118                 ))}
   119               </SelectContent>
   120             </Select>
   121           </div>
   122         </CardContent>
   123       </Card>
   124 
   125       {/* 职位列表 */}
   126       <div className="space-y-1">
   127         <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">共找到 {jobs.length} 个职位</p>
   128       </div>
   129 
   130       {loading ? (
   131         <div className="space-y-3">
   132           {Array(5).fill(0).map((_, i) => (
   133             <Card key={i}><CardContent className="p-4 space-y-2">
   134               <Skeleton className="h-5 w-1/2 bg-muted" />
   135               <Skeleton className="h-4 w-1/3 bg-muted" />
   136             </CardContent></Card>
   137           ))}
   138         </div>
   139       ) : jobs.length === 0 ? (
   140         <Card><CardContent className="py-16 text-center text-muted-foreground">
   141           暂无符合条件的职位，请调整筛选条件
   142         </CardContent></Card>
   143       ) : (
   144         <div className="space-y-3">
   145           {jobs.map(job => (
   146             <Link key={job.id} to={`/jobseeker/jobs/${job.id}`}>
   147               <Card className="hover:shadow-md transition-shadow">
   148                 <CardContent className="p-4">
   149                   <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
   150                     <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 space-y-1.5">
   151                       <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
   152                         <h3 className="font-semibold text-foreground truncate">{job.title}</h3>
   153                         <Badge variant="outline" className="text-xs shrink-0">{job.industry || '通用'}</Badge>
   154                       </div>
   155                       <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
   156                         {job.location && <span className="flex items-center gap-1 whitespace-nowrap"><MapPin className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />{job.location}</span>}
   157                         <span className="flex items-center gap-1 whitespace-nowrap"><DollarSign className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />{formatSalary(job.salary_min, job.salary_max)}</span>
   158                         <span className="flex items-center gap-1 whitespace-nowrap"><Clock className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />{job.job_type}</span>
   159                         {job.experience_required && <span className="whitespace-nowrap">{job.experience_required}</span>}
   160                       </div>
   161                       {Array.isArray(job.skills_required) && job.skills_required.length > 0 && (
   162                         <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1 pt-1">
   163                           {(job.skills_required as string[]).slice(0, 5).map((s: string) => (
   164                             <Badge key={s} variant="secondary" className="text-xs">{s}</Badge>
   165                           ))}
   166                         </div>
   167                       )}
   168                     </div>
   169                     <ChevronRight className="w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground shrink-0 mt-1" />
   170                   </div>
   171                 </CardContent>
   172               </Card>
   173             </Link>
   174           ))}
   175         </div>
   176       )}
   177     </div>
   178   );
   179 }

     1 import React, { useMemo } from 'react';
     2 import { TreeNode } from '@/types/types';
     3 
     4 // ─── 颜色配置（蓝色系）───────────────────────────────────────────
     5 const NODE_COLORS = [
     6   { fill: '#1A4FA8', text: '#ffffff', stroke: '#1A4FA8' }, // 根节点：深蓝
     7   { fill: '#2563EB', text: '#ffffff', stroke: '#2563EB' }, // 一级：亮蓝
     8   { fill: '#3B82F6', text: '#ffffff', stroke: '#3B82F6' }, // 二级：中蓝
     9   { fill: '#DBEAFE', text: '#1e3a8a', stroke: '#93C5FD' }, // 三级：浅蓝
    10 ];
    11 
    12 const EDGE_COLOR = '#BFDBFE';
    13 const BAR_BG = '#E0EFFE';
    14 const BAR_FG_HIGH = '#1A4FA8';
    15 const BAR_FG_MID = '#3B82F6';
    16 const BAR_FG_LOW = '#93C5FD';
    17 const VALUE_COLOR = '#1e3a8a';
    18 
    19 // ─── 布局常量 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    20 const NODE_W = 90;     // 节点宽
    21 const NODE_H = 32;     // 节点高
    22 const RADIUS = 8;      // 圆角
    23 const H_GAP = 20;      // 同层节点水平间距
    24 const V_GAP = 60;      // 层间垂直间距
    25 const LEAF_BAR_H = 8;  // 叶子节点值条高度
    26 const PADDING = 16;    // 整体边距
    27 
    28 // ─── 布局计算 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    29 interface LayoutNode {
    30   node: TreeNode;
    31   x: number;       // 中心 x
    32   y: number;       // 顶部 y
    33   depth: number;
    34   width: number;   // 子树宽度
    35   children: LayoutNode[];
    36 }
    37 
    38 function calcLeafWidth(node: TreeNode): number {
    39   if (!node.children || node.children.length === 0) return NODE_W;
    40   return node.children.reduce((sum, c) => sum + calcLeafWidth(c) + H_GAP, -H_GAP);
    41 }
    42 
    43 function buildLayout(node: TreeNode, depth: number, offsetX: number): LayoutNode {
    44   const subtreeW = calcLeafWidth(node);
    45   const cx = offsetX + subtreeW / 2;
    46   const y = PADDING + depth * (NODE_H + V_GAP);
    47 
    48   if (!node.children || node.children.length === 0) {
    49     return { node, x: cx, y, depth, width: subtreeW, children: [] };
    50   }
    51 
    52   let childX = offsetX;
    53   const children: LayoutNode[] = node.children.map(child => {
    54     const cw = calcLeafWidth(child);
    55     const laid = buildLayout(child, depth + 1, childX);
    56     childX += cw + H_GAP;
    57     return laid;
    58   });
    59 
    60   return { node, x: cx, y, depth, width: subtreeW, children };
    61 }
    62 
    63 function collectNodes(layout: LayoutNode, acc: LayoutNode[] = []): LayoutNode[] {
    64   acc.push(layout);
    65   layout.children.forEach(c => collectNodes(c, acc));
    66   return acc;
    67 }
    68 
    69 function collectEdges(layout: LayoutNode, acc: { from: LayoutNode; to: LayoutNode }[] = []) {
    70   layout.children.forEach(c => {
    71     acc.push({ from: layout, to: c });
    72     collectEdges(c, acc);
    73   });
    74   return acc;
    75 }
    76 
    77 // ─── 单节点渲染 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    78 function NodeRect({ layout }: { layout: LayoutNode }) {
    79   const { node, x, y, depth } = layout;
    80   const color = NODE_COLORS[Math.min(depth, NODE_COLORS.length - 1)];
    81   const nx = x - NODE_W / 2;
    82   const isLeaf = !node.children || node.children.length === 0;
    83   const hasValue = isLeaf && node.value !== undefined;
    84 
    85   const barFill =
    86     node.value !== undefined
    87       ? node.value >= 75 ? BAR_FG_HIGH
    88         : node.value >= 50 ? BAR_FG_MID
    89         : BAR_FG_LOW
    90       : BAR_FG_LOW;
    91 
    92   const barWidth = hasValue ? Math.round((node.value! / 100) * (NODE_W - 16)) : 0;
    93 
    94   return (
    95     <g>
    96       {/* 节点背景 */}
    97       <rect
    98         x={nx}
    99         y={y}
   100         width={NODE_W}
   101         height={NODE_H}
   102         rx={RADIUS}
   103         ry={RADIUS}
   104         fill={color.fill}
   105         stroke={color.stroke}
   106         strokeWidth={1.5}
   107       />
   108       {/* 节点标签 */}
   109       <text
   110         x={x}
   111         y={y + (hasValue ? 12 : NODE_H / 2 + 4.5)}
   112         textAnchor="middle"
   113         fontSize={depth === 0 ? 12 : 11}
   114         fontWeight={depth <= 1 ? 600 : 400}
   115         fill={color.text}
   116         fontFamily="Inter, system-ui, sans-serif"
   117       >
   118         {node.name.length > 7 ? node.name.slice(0, 6) + '…' : node.name}
   119       </text>
   120       {/* 能力值条 */}
   121       {hasValue && (
   122         <>
   123           <rect
   124             x={nx + 8}
   125             y={y + NODE_H - LEAF_BAR_H - 4}
   126             width={NODE_W - 16}
   127             height={LEAF_BAR_H}
   128             rx={3}
   129             fill={BAR_BG}
   130           />
   131           <rect
   132             x={nx + 8}
   133             y={y + NODE_H - LEAF_BAR_H - 4}
   134             width={barWidth}
   135             height={LEAF_BAR_H}
   136             rx={3}
   137             fill={barFill}
   138           />
   139           <text
   140             x={nx + NODE_W + 3}
   141             y={y + NODE_H - 4}
   142             fontSize={9}
   143             fill={VALUE_COLOR}
   144             fontFamily="Inter, system-ui, sans-serif"
   145           >
   146             {node.value}
   147           </text>
   148         </>
   149       )}
   150     </g>
   151   );
   152 }
   153 
   154 // ─── 连线（贝塞尔曲线）────────────────────────────────────────────
   155 function Edge({ from, to }: { from: LayoutNode; to: LayoutNode }) {
   156   const x1 = from.x;
   157   const y1 = from.y + NODE_H;
   158   const x2 = to.x;
   159   const y2 = to.y;
   160   const cy1 = y1 + (y2 - y1) * 0.5;
   161   const cy2 = y1 + (y2 - y1) * 0.5;
   162   return (
   163     <path
   164       d={`M ${x1} ${y1} C ${x1} ${cy1}, ${x2} ${cy2}, ${x2} ${y2}`}
   165       fill="none"
   166       stroke={EDGE_COLOR}
   167       strokeWidth={1.5}
   168       strokeLinecap="round"
   169     />
   170   );
   171 }
   172 
   173 // ─── 主组件 ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   174 interface CapabilityTreeImageProps {
   175   data: TreeNode;
   176   className?: string;
   177 }
   178 
   179 export function CapabilityTreeImage({ data, className = '' }: CapabilityTreeImageProps) {
   180   const { layout, svgWidth, svgHeight } = useMemo(() => {
   181     const layout = buildLayout(data, 0, PADDING);
   182     const allNodes = collectNodes(layout);
   183     // 计算画布尺寸
   184     const maxX = Math.max(...allNodes.map(n => n.x + NODE_W / 2 + PADDING));
   185     const maxY = Math.max(...allNodes.map(n => n.y + NODE_H + PADDING + (n.node.value !== undefined ? 14 : 0)));
   186     return {
   187       layout,
   188       svgWidth: Math.max(maxX + PADDING, 280),
   189       svgHeight: Math.max(maxY + PADDING, 120),
   190     };
   191   }, [data]);
   192 
   193   const allNodes = collectNodes(layout);
   194   const allEdges = collectEdges(layout);
   195 
   196   return (
   197     <div className={`w-full overflow-x-auto ${className}`}>
   198       <svg
   199         viewBox={`0 0 ${svgWidth} ${svgHeight}`}
   200         width="100%"
   201         style={{ minWidth: Math.min(svgWidth, 280), maxWidth: svgWidth, display: 'block' }}
   202         aria-label="能力树图"
   203         role="img"
   204       >
   205         {/* 背景 */}
   206         <rect width={svgWidth} height={svgHeight} fill="#F0F7FF" rx={12} />
   207         {/* 连线（先渲染，在节点下层） */}
   208         <g>
   209           {allEdges.map((e, i) => (
   210             <Edge key={i} from={e.from} to={e.to} />
   211           ))}
   212         </g>
   213         {/* 节点 */}
   214         <g>
   215           {allNodes.map((n, i) => (
   216             <NodeRect key={i} layout={n} />
   217           ))}
   218         </g>
   219       </svg>
   220     </div>
   221   );
   222 }

```
// Edge Function: parse-resume-capability
// 解析简历文本，通过文心大模型生成能力雷达图数据和能力树数据（SSE 流式）
const corsHeaders = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type",
};

const SYSTEM_PROMPT = `你是一名专业的HR顾问和能力评估专家。请根据用户提供的简历内容，分析候选人的综合能力，并输出结构化的能力图谱数据。

输出要求（严格JSON格式，不输出任何其他内容）：
{
  "radar_data": {
    "技术能力": 85,
    "项目经验": 75,
    "学习能力": 80,
    "沟通协作": 70,
    "问题解决": 78,
    "领导力": 60
  },
  "tree_data": {
    "name": "核心能力",
    "children": [
      {
        "name": "技术栈",
        "children": [
          {"name": "Python", "value": 85},
          {"name": "React", "value": 78}
        ]
      },
      {
        "name": "软技能",
        "children": [
          {"name": "沟通表达", "value": 75},
          {"name": "团队协作", "value": 80}
        ]
      }
    ]
  },
  "summary": "该候选人具有扎实的技术背景，在XX领域有丰富经验...",
  "industry": "tech"
}

评分说明：
- 所有分值范围 0-100
- 根据简历内容真实评估，不要虚高
- radar_data 必须包含 6 个维度，可根据简历内容选择最合适的维度名称
- tree_data 根节点下最多 4 个分支，每个分支下 2-6 个叶节点（带value）
- industry 从以下选择：tech / finance / manufacturing / education / medical / other`;

Deno.serve(async (req: Request): Promise<Response> => {
  if (req.method === "OPTIONS") return new Response(null, { headers: corsHeaders });
  if (req.method !== "POST") return new Response("Method Not Allowed", { status: 405, headers: corsHeaders });

  let resumeText: string;
  let resumeTitle: string;

  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    resumeText = body.resume_text ?? "";
    resumeTitle = body.resume_title ?? "简历";
    if (!resumeText.trim()) throw new Error("resume_text is required");
  } catch (err) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: `Invalid request: ${(err as Error).message}` }),
      { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );
  }

  const apiKey = Deno.env.get("INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY");
  if (!apiKey) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: "Server configuration error" }),
      { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );
  }

  const messages = [
    { role: "system", content: SYSTEM_PROMPT },
    {
      role: "user",
      content: `请分析以下简历内容，生成能力图谱数据：\n\n【简历标题】${resumeTitle}\n\n【简历内容】\n${resumeText.slice(0, 8000)}`,
    },
  ];

  const upstream = await fetch(
    "https://app-bhs9a5otro5d-api-zYkZz8qovQ1L-gateway.appmiaoda.com/v2/chat/completions",
    {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
        "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({ messages, enable_thinking: false }),
    }
  );

  if (!upstream.ok || !upstream.body) {
    const errText = await upstream.text().catch(() => "");
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: `Upstream error: ${upstream.status}`, detail: errText }),
      { status: 502, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );
  }

  // 透传 SSE 流
  return new Response(upstream.body, {
    headers: {
      ...corsHeaders,
      "Content-Type": "text/event-stream",
      "Cache-Control": "no-cache",
      "Connection": "keep-alive",
    },
  });
});

New String: ```
import React, { useCallback, useRef, useState } from 'react';

interface RadarDataItem {
  subject: string;
  value: number;
  fullMark?: number;
}

interface CapabilityRadarChartProps {
  data: RadarDataItem[];
  color?: string;
  compareData?: RadarDataItem[];
  compareColor?: string;
  height?: number;
  /** 可编辑模式（拖拽调整值）*/
  editable?: boolean;
  onChange?: (data: RadarDataItem[]) => void;
}

const SIZE = 280;       // SVG 尺寸
const CX = SIZE / 2;   // 中心 x
const CY = SIZE / 2;   // 中心 y
const R = 105;          // 最大半径
const LEVELS = 5;       // 同心圆层数
const HANDLE_R = 8;    // 拖拽点半径

function polarToXY(angle: number, radius: number) {
  const rad = (angle - 90) * (Math.PI / 180);
  return { x: CX + radius * Math.cos(rad), y: CY + radius * Math.sin(rad) };
}

function valueToRadius(value: number) {
  return (Math.max(0, Math.min(100, value)) / 100) * R;
}

function xyToValue(angle: number, mx: number, my: number) {
  const rad = (angle - 90) * (Math.PI / 180);
  // Project (mx-CX, my-CY) onto axis direction
  const dot = (mx - CX) * Math.cos(rad) + (my - CY) * Math.sin(rad);
  return Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Math.round((dot / R) * 100)));
}

export function CapabilityRadarChart({
  data,
  color = 'hsl(217, 72%, 38%)',
  compareData,
  compareColor = 'hsl(22, 89%, 54%)',
  height = 300,
  editable = false,
  onChange,
}: CapabilityRadarChartProps) {
  const [localData, setLocalData] = useState<RadarDataItem[]>(data);
  const [draggingIdx, setDraggingIdx] = useState<number | null>(null);
  const [hoveredIdx, setHoveredIdx] = useState<number | null>(null);
  const svgRef = useRef<SVGSVGElement>(null);

  // 当 data prop 变化时同步
  const prevDataRef = useRef(data);
  if (data !== prevDataRef.current) {
    prevDataRef.current = data;
    setLocalData(data);
  }

  const activeData = editable ? localData : data;
  const n = activeData.length;
  const angleStep = 360 / n;

  const getSVGPoint = useCallback((e: React.MouseEvent | React.TouchEvent) => {
    const svg = svgRef.current;
    if (!svg) return { x: 0, y: 0 };
    const rect = svg.getBoundingClientRect();
    const clientX = 'touches' in e ? e.touches[0].clientX : (e as React.MouseEvent).clientX;
    const clientY = 'touches' in e ? e.touches[0].clientY : (e as React.MouseEvent).clientY;
    const scaleX = SIZE / rect.width;
    const scaleY = SIZE / rect.height;
    return { x: (clientX - rect.left) * scaleX, y: (clientY - rect.top) * scaleY };
  }, []);

  const handleDragMove = useCallback((e: React.MouseEvent | React.TouchEvent) => {
    if (!editable || draggingIdx === null) return;
    e.preventDefault();
    const { x, y } = getSVGPoint(e);
    const angle = draggingIdx * angleStep;
    const newVal = xyToValue(angle, x, y);
    setLocalData(prev => {
      const next = prev.map((d, i) => i === draggingIdx ? { ...d, value: newVal } : d);
      onChange?.(next);
      return next;
    });
  }, [editable, draggingIdx, angleStep, getSVGPoint, onChange]);

  const handleDragEnd = useCallback(() => {
    setDraggingIdx(null);
  }, []);

  // 构建多边形顶点
  const polyPoints = activeData.map((d, i) => {
    const { x, y } = polarToXY(i * angleStep, valueToRadius(d.value));
    return `${x},${y}`;
  }).join(' ');

  const comparePoints = compareData
    ? compareData.map((d, i) => {
        const { x, y } = polarToXY(i * angleStep, valueToRadius(d.value));
        return `${x},${y}`;
      }).join(' ')
    : null;

  return (
    <div className="w-full min-w-0 overflow-hidden flex flex-col items-center gap-2">
      <svg
        ref={svgRef}
        viewBox={`0 0 ${SIZE} ${SIZE}`}
        width="100%"
        style={{ maxWidth: height, display: 'block', touchAction: editable ? 'none' : 'auto' }}
        onMouseMove={handleDragMove}
        onMouseUp={handleDragEnd}
        onMouseLeave={handleDragEnd}
        onTouchMove={handleDragMove}
        onTouchEnd={handleDragEnd}
      >
        {/* 同心圆网格 */}
        {Array.from({ length: LEVELS }).map((_, lvl) => (
          <polygon
            key={lvl}
            points={activeData.map((_, i) => {
              const { x, y } = polarToXY(i * angleStep, R * ((lvl + 1) / LEVELS));
              return `${x},${y}`;
            }).join(' ')}
            fill="none"
            stroke="hsl(var(--border))"
            strokeWidth={0.8}
            opacity={0.6}
          />
        ))}

        {/* 轴线 */}
        {activeData.map((_, i) => {
          const { x, y } = polarToXY(i * angleStep, R);
          return <line key={i} x1={CX} y1={CY} x2={x} y2={y} stroke="hsl(var(--border))" strokeWidth={0.8} opacity={0.5} />;
        })}

        {/* 刻度文字（外层） */}
        {activeData.map((d, i) => {
          const { x, y } = polarToXY(i * angleStep, R + 18);
          return (
            <text
              key={i}
              x={x}
              y={y}
              textAnchor="middle"
              dominantBaseline="middle"
              fontSize={10}
              fill="hsl(var(--muted-foreground))"
              fontFamily="system-ui, sans-serif"
            >
              {d.subject}
            </text>
          );
        })}

        {/* 对比多边形（底层） */}
        {comparePoints && (
          <polygon
            points={comparePoints}
            fill={compareColor}
            fillOpacity={0.12}
            stroke={compareColor}
            strokeWidth={1.5}
            strokeLinejoin="round"
          />
        )}

        {/* 主数据多边形 */}
        <polygon
          points={polyPoints}
          fill={color}
          fillOpacity={0.2}
          stroke={color}
          strokeWidth={2}
          strokeLinejoin="round"
        />

        {/* 拖拽点 */}
        {editable && activeData.map((d, i) => {
          const angle = i * angleStep;
          const { x, y } = polarToXY(angle, valueToRadius(d.value));
          const isDragging = draggingIdx === i;
          const isHovered = hoveredIdx === i;
          return (
            <g key={i}>
              {/* 拖拽时显示轴向辅助线 */}
              {isDragging && (() => {
                const { x: ax, y: ay } = polarToXY(angle, R);
                return <line x1={CX} y1={CY} x2={ax} y2={ay} stroke={color} strokeWidth={1.5} strokeDasharray="4 3" opacity={0.5} />;
              })()}
              {/* 值标签 */}
              {(isDragging || isHovered) && (() => {
                const { x: lx, y: ly } = polarToXY(angle, valueToRadius(d.value) + 16);
                return (
                  <text x={lx} y={ly} textAnchor="middle" dominantBaseline="middle" fontSize={9} fontWeight={600} fill={color} fontFamily="system-ui, sans-serif">
                    {d.value}
                  </text>
                );
              })()}
              {/* 拖拽手柄 */}
              <circle
                cx={x} cy={y}
                r={isDragging ? HANDLE_R + 2 : HANDLE_R}
                fill={isDragging ? color : 'hsl(var(--background))'}
                stroke={color}
                strokeWidth={2}
                style={{ cursor: 'grab', userSelect: 'none' }}
                onMouseDown={e => { e.preventDefault(); setDraggingIdx(i); }}
                onMouseEnter={() => setHoveredIdx(i)}
                onMouseLeave={() => !isDragging && setHoveredIdx(null)}
                onTouchStart={e => { e.preventDefault(); setDraggingIdx(i); }}
              />
            </g>
          );
        })}

        {/* 非编辑模式：数据点 */}
        {!editable && activeData.map((d, i) => {
          const { x, y } = polarToXY(i * angleStep, valueToRadius(d.value));
          return <circle key={i} cx={x} cy={y} r={3.5} fill={color} stroke="hsl(var(--background))" strokeWidth={1.5} />;
        })}
      </svg>

      {/* 图例（有对比数据时显示） */}
      {compareData && (
        <div className="flex items-center gap-4 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
          <span className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
            <span className="w-3 h-3 rounded-sm inline-block" style={{ background: color, opacity: 0.6 }} />
            个人能力
          </span>
          <span className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
            <span className="w-3 h-3 rounded-sm inline-block" style={{ background: compareColor, opacity: 0.4 }} />
            岗位要求
          </span>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 编辑模式下的数值摘要 */}
      {editable && (
        <div className="w-full flex flex-wrap gap-x-4 gap-y-1 justify-center mt-1">
          {activeData.map(d => (
            <span key={d.subject} className="text-xs text-muted-foreground whitespace-nowrap">
              <span className="font-medium text-foreground">{d.subject}</span>
              <span className="ml-1" style={{ color }}>
                {d.value}
              </span>
            </span>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { TreeNode } from '@/types/types';
import { ChevronRight, ChevronDown, Circle } from 'lucide-react';

interface CapabilityTreeChartProps {
  data: TreeNode;
  depth?: number;
}

interface TreeNodeItemProps {
  node: TreeNode;
  depth: number;
  expanded?: boolean;
}

function TreeNodeItem({ node, depth }: TreeNodeItemProps) {
  const [isExpanded, setIsExpanded] = useState(depth < 2);
  const hasChildren = node.children && node.children.length > 0;
  const indent = depth * 20;

  const getNodeColor = () => {
    if (depth === 0) return 'text-primary font-semibold text-base';
    if (depth === 1) return 'text-foreground font-medium';
    return 'text-muted-foreground text-sm';
  };

  const getBarColor = () => {
    if (node.value === undefined) return null;
    if (node.value >= 80) return 'bg-primary';
    if (node.value >= 60) return 'bg-chart-2';
    if (node.value >= 40) return 'bg-chart-4';

    <div>
      <div
        className={`flex items-center gap-2 py-1.5 rounded-sm hover:bg-muted/50 cursor-pointer transition-colors ${hasChildren ? '' : 'cursor-default'}`}
        style={{ paddingLeft: `${indent + 8}px` }}
        onClick={() => hasChildren && setIsExpanded(v => !v)}
      >
        <span className="shrink-0 w-4 h-4 flex items-center justify-center">
          {hasChildren ? (
            isExpanded ? <ChevronDown className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground" /> : <ChevronRight className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground" />

          )}
        </span>
        <span className={`flex-1 min-w-0 truncate ${getNodeColor()}`}>{node.name}</span>
        {node.value !== undefined && (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0">
            <div className="w-20 h-1.5 bg-muted rounded-full overflow-hidden">
              <div
                className={`h-full rounded-full transition-all ${getBarColor()}`}
                style={{ width: `${node.value}%` }}
              />
            </div>
            <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground w-7 text-right">{node.value}</span>
          </div>

      </div>

        <div>
          {node.children!.map((child, i) => (
            <TreeNodeItem key={i} node={child} depth={depth + 1} />
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

export function CapabilityTreeChart({ data, depth = 0 }: CapabilityTreeChartProps) {
  return (
    <div className="w-full">
      <TreeNodeItem node={data} depth={depth} />

}

New String: ```
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { TreeNode } from '@/types/types';
import { ChevronRight, ChevronDown, Circle, GripVertical } from 'lucide-react';

interface CapabilityTreeChartProps {
  data: TreeNode;
  depth?: number;
  /** 可编辑模式：叶节点支持拖拽调整值 */
  editable?: boolean;
  onChange?: (newData: TreeNode) => void;
}

interface TreeNodeItemProps {
  node: TreeNode;
  depth: number;
  editable: boolean;
  onLeafChange?: (name: string, value: number) => void;
}

function getBarColor(value?: number) {
  if (value === undefined) return null;
  if (value >= 80) return 'bg-primary';
  if (value >= 60) return 'bg-chart-2';
  if (value >= 40) return 'bg-chart-4';
  return 'bg-muted-foreground';
}

function deepUpdate(node: TreeNode, leafName: string, newValue: number): TreeNode {
  if (!node.children || node.children.length === 0) {
    return node.name === leafName ? { ...node, value: newValue } : node;
  }
  return { ...node, children: node.children.map(c => deepUpdate(c, leafName, newValue)) };
}

function TreeNodeItem({ node, depth, editable, onLeafChange }: TreeNodeItemProps) {
  const [isExpanded, setIsExpanded] = useState(depth < 2);
  const [dragging, setDragging] = useState(false);
  const hasChildren = node.children && node.children.length > 0;
  const isLeaf = !hasChildren;
  const indent = depth * 20;
  const barColor = getBarColor(node.value);

  // 拖拽调整值
  const handleBarDrag = (e: React.MouseEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
    if (!editable || !isLeaf || node.value === undefined) return;
    const barEl = e.currentTarget;
    const rect = barEl.getBoundingClientRect();
    setDragging(true);

    const update = (clientX: number) => {
      const ratio = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, (clientX - rect.left) / rect.width));
      onLeafChange?.(node.name, Math.round(ratio * 100));
    };
    update(e.clientX);

    const onMove = (ev: MouseEvent) => update(ev.clientX);
    const onUp = () => {
      setDragging(false);
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', onMove);
      window.removeEventListener('mouseup', onUp);
    };
    window.addEventListener('mousemove', onMove);
    window.addEventListener('mouseup', onUp);
  };

  // 触摸拖拽
  const handleBarTouchDrag = (e: React.TouchEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
    if (!editable || !isLeaf || node.value === undefined) return;
    const barEl = e.currentTarget;
    const rect = barEl.getBoundingClientRect();
    setDragging(true);

    const update = (clientX: number) => {
      const ratio = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, (clientX - rect.left) / rect.width));
      onLeafChange?.(node.name, Math.round(ratio * 100));
    };

    const onMove = (ev: TouchEvent) => { ev.preventDefault(); update(ev.touches[0].clientX); };
    const onEnd = () => {
      setDragging(false);
      window.removeEventListener('touchmove', onMove);
      window.removeEventListener('touchend', onEnd);
    };
    window.addEventListener('touchmove', onMove, { passive: false });
    window.addEventListener('touchend', onEnd);
  };

  const getNodeColor = () => {
    if (depth === 0) return 'text-primary font-semibold text-base';
    if (depth === 1) return 'text-foreground font-medium';
    return 'text-muted-foreground text-sm';
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <div
        className={`flex items-center gap-2 py-1.5 rounded-sm transition-colors ${
          hasChildren ? 'hover:bg-muted/50 cursor-pointer' : 'cursor-default'
        }`}
        style={{ paddingLeft: `${indent + 8}px` }}
        onClick={() => hasChildren && setIsExpanded(v => !v)}
      >
        <span className="shrink-0 w-4 h-4 flex items-center justify-center">
          {hasChildren ? (
            isExpanded
              ? <ChevronDown className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground" />
              : <ChevronRight className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground" />
          ) : (
            <Circle className="w-2 h-2 text-muted-foreground fill-muted-foreground" />
          )}
        </span>
        <span className={`flex-1 min-w-0 truncate ${getNodeColor()}`}>{node.name}</span>

        {node.value !== undefined && (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0 pr-2">
            {/* 可拖拽进度条 */}
            <div
              className={`relative w-24 h-3 bg-muted rounded-full overflow-hidden ${
                editable && isLeaf ? 'cursor-ew-resize select-none' : ''
              } ${dragging ? 'ring-1 ring-primary' : ''}`}
              onMouseDown={editable && isLeaf ? handleBarDrag : undefined}
              onTouchStart={editable && isLeaf ? handleBarTouchDrag : undefined}
              title={editable && isLeaf ? '拖拽调整能力值' : undefined}
            >
              <div
                className={`h-full rounded-full transition-all ${barColor ?? 'bg-muted-foreground'}`}
                style={{ width: `${node.value}%` }}
              />
              {/* 编辑模式拖拽手柄标识 */}
              {editable && isLeaf && (
                <div
                  className="absolute top-0 h-full flex items-center pointer-events-none"
                  style={{ left: `${Math.max(0, node.value - 8)}%` }}
                >
                  <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-background border border-primary opacity-80" />
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
            <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground w-7 text-right tabular-nums">
              {node.value}
            </span>
            {editable && isLeaf && (
              <GripVertical className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground/40 shrink-0" />
            )}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {hasChildren && isExpanded && (
        <div>
          {node.children!.map((child, i) => (
            <TreeNodeItem
              key={i}
              node={child}
              depth={depth + 1}
              editable={editable}
              onLeafChange={onLeafChange}
            />
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

export function CapabilityTreeChart({ data, depth = 0, editable = false, onChange }: CapabilityTreeChartProps) {
  const handleLeafChange = (leafName: string, value: number) => {
    const updated = deepUpdate(data, leafName, value);
    onChange?.(updated);
  };

  return (
    <div className="w-full">
      {editable && (
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-2 flex items-center gap-1">
          <GripVertical className="w-3 h-3" />
          拖拽蓝色进度条可调整技能掌握程度
        </p>
      )}
      <TreeNodeItem
        node={data}
        depth={depth}
        editable={editable}
        onLeafChange={handleLeafChange}
      />
    </div>
  );
}

New String: ```
  const handleSaveCapability = async () => {
    const radarObj: Record<string, number> = {};
    radarData.forEach(item => { radarObj[item.subject] = item.value; });

    const currentTemplate = templates.find(t => t.industry === selectedIndustry);
    const treeToSave = (treeDataEditable && Object.keys(treeDataEditable).length > 0)
      ? treeDataEditable
      : currentTemplate?.skill_tree ?? DEFAULT_TREE;

    if (capability) {
      await supabase.from('capability_data')
        .update({ radar_data: radarObj, tree_data: treeToSave, industry: selectedIndustry })
        .eq('id', capability.id);
    } else {
      await supabase.from('capability_data').insert({
        profile_id: user!.id,
        industry: selectedIndustry,
        radar_data: radarObj,
        tree_data: treeToSave,
        skills: radarData.map(r => ({ name: r.subject, level: r.value })),
      });
    }
    toast.success('能力数据已保存');
    fetchCapabilityData();
  };

  // AI 解析简历 → 生成能力图谱
  const handleAiParseResume = async () => {
    // 找主简历或第一份有内容的简历
    const targetResume = resumes.find(r => r.is_primary) ?? resumes[0];
    if (!targetResume) {
      toast.info('请先创建简历再使用 AI 解析');
      return;
    }

    // 构建简历文本（从结构化字段拼接）
    let resumeText = '';
    if (targetResume.parsed_content) {
      resumeText = targetResume.parsed_content;
    } else {
      // 从结构化数据生成文本
      const parts: string[] = [`简历标题：${targetResume.title}`];
      if (targetResume.summary) parts.push(`个人简介：${targetResume.summary}`);
      if (Array.isArray(targetResume.education) && targetResume.education.length > 0) {
        parts.push('教育经历：' + targetResume.education.map(e =>
          `${e.school} ${e.degree} ${e.major} (${e.start_year}-${e.end_year})`
        ).join('；'));
      }
      if (Array.isArray(targetResume.experience) && targetResume.experience.length > 0) {
        parts.push('工作经历：' + targetResume.experience.map(e =>
          `${e.company} ${e.title}：${e.description} (${e.start_date}-${e.end_date})`
        ).join('；'));
      }
      if (Array.isArray(targetResume.skills) && targetResume.skills.length > 0) {
        parts.push('技能：' + targetResume.skills.map(s => `${s.name}(${s.level})`).join('、'));
      }
      resumeText = parts.join('\n');
    }

    if (!resumeText.trim() || resumeText === `简历标题：${targetResume.title}`) {
      toast.info('简历内容暂为空，请先填写工作经历、技能或上传文件后再 AI 解析');
      return;
    }

    setAiParsing(true);
    setAiParseProgress('');
    aiAbortRef.current?.abort();
    aiAbortRef.current = new AbortController();

    const SUPABASE_URL = import.meta.env.VITE_SUPABASE_URL as string;
    const SUPABASE_ANON_KEY = import.meta.env.VITE_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY as string;

    let fullText = '';
    try {
      const resp = await fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/functions/v1/parse-resume-capability`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
          'Authorization': `Bearer ${SUPABASE_ANON_KEY}`,
          'apikey': SUPABASE_ANON_KEY,
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({ resume_text: resumeText, resume_title: targetResume.title }),
        signal: aiAbortRef.current.signal,
      });

      if (!resp.ok || !resp.body) throw new Error(`HTTP ${resp.status}`);

      const reader = resp.body.getReader();
      const decoder = new TextDecoder();
      const parser = createParser({
        onEvent: (event) => {
          if (event.data === '[DONE]') return;
          try {
            const parsed = JSON.parse(event.data);
            const chunk = parsed.choices?.[0]?.delta?.content ?? '';
            if (chunk) {
              fullText += chunk;
              setAiParseProgress(fullText);
            }
          } catch { /* skip */ }
        },
      });

      const read = async (): Promise<void> => {
        const { done, value } = await reader.read();
        if (done) return;
        parser.feed(decoder.decode(value, { stream: true }));
        return read();
      };
      await read();

      // 提取 JSON
      const jsonMatch = fullText.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/);
      if (!jsonMatch) throw new Error('AI 返回内容格式错误');
      const parsed = JSON.parse(jsonMatch[0]);

      // 更新雷达图数据
      if (parsed.radar_data && typeof parsed.radar_data === 'object') {
        const newRadar = Object.entries(parsed.radar_data as Record<string, number>)
          .map(([subject, value]) => ({ subject, value: Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Math.round(value))) }));
        if (newRadar.length > 0) setRadarData(newRadar);
      }

      // 更新能力树数据
      if (parsed.tree_data && typeof parsed.tree_data === 'object') {
        setTreeDataEditable(parsed.tree_data as TreeNode);
      }

      // 更新行业
      if (parsed.industry) setSelectedIndustry(parsed.industry);

      setAiParseProgress('');
      toast.success('AI 能力图谱已生成，点击"保存图谱"持久化数据');
    } catch (err: unknown) {
      if ((err as Error).name !== 'AbortError') {
        console.error('AI 解析失败:', err);
        toast.error('AI 解析失败，请稍后重试');
      }
      setAiParseProgress('');
    } finally {
      setAiParsing(false);
    }
  };

   444                             {formatFileSize(resume.file_size)}
   445                           </span>
   446                         )}
   447                         <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
   448                           {new Date(resume.updated_at).toLocaleDateString('zh-CN')}
   449                         </span>
   450                       </div>
   451                     </div>
   452 
   453                     {/* 操作区 */}
   454                     <div className="flex items-center gap-1 shrink-0">
   455                       {/* 上传/替换文件 */}
   456                       <Button
   457                         variant="ghost"
   458                         size="icon"
   459                         className="h-8 w-8 text-muted-foreground hover:text-primary"
   460                         title={resume.file_url ? '替换文件' : '上传文件'}
   461                         onClick={() => setUploadingResumeId(
   462                           uploadingResumeId === resume.id ? null : resume.id
   463                         )}
   464                       >
   465                         <Upload className="w-4 h-4" />
   466                       </Button>
   467                       {/* 下载 */}
   468                       {resume.file_url && (
   469                         <Button
   470                           variant="ghost"
   471                           size="icon"
   472                           className="h-8 w-8 text-muted-foreground hover:text-primary"
   473                           title="下载文件"
   474                           onClick={() => handleDownload(resume)}
   475                         >
   476                           <Download className="w-4 h-4" />
   477                         </Button>
   478                       )}
   479                       {/* 设为主简历 */}
   480                       {!resume.is_primary && (
   481                         <Button
   482                           variant="ghost"
   483                           size="icon"
   484                           className="h-8 w-8 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
   485                           title="设为主简历"
   486                           onClick={() => handleSetPrimary(resume.id)}
   487                         >
   488                           <Star className="w-4 h-4" />
   489                         </Button>
   490                       )}
   491                       {/* 删除 */}
   492                       <AlertDialog>
   493                         <AlertDialogTrigger asChild>
   494                           <Button
   495                             variant="ghost"
   496                             size="icon"
   497                             className="h-8 w-8 text-destructive hover:text-destructive"
   498                           >
   499                             <Trash2 className="w-4 h-4" />
   500                           </Button>
   501                         </AlertDialogTrigger>
   502                         <AlertDialogContent className="max-w-[calc(100%-2rem)] md:max-w-lg">
   503                           <AlertDialogHeader>
   504                             <AlertDialogTitle>确认删除简历</AlertDialogTitle>
   505                             <AlertDialogDescription>

   507                             </AlertDialogDescription>

   514                             >
   515                               确认删除
   516                             </AlertDialogAction>
   517                           </AlertDialogFooter>
   518                         </AlertDialogContent>
   519                       </AlertDialog>
   520                     </div>
   521                   </div>
   522 
   523                   {/* 展开的上传区域 */}
   524                   {uploadingResumeId === resume.id && (
   525                     <div className="border-t border-border bg-muted/20 p-4">
   526                       <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-3">
   527                         {resume.file_url ? '替换已有文件（原文件将被覆盖）' : '上传简历文件'}
   528                       </p>
   529                       <ResumeUploader
   530                         resumeId={resume.id}
